The recovery proceedings in respect of these defaulters are pending as on 31.12.2025. Any person having information about the assets or immovable properties of any of these defaulters may forward the information to Recovery Officer, SEBI at the address: The Recovery Officer,  Recovery and Refunds Department, SEBI Bhavan-II, Plot No. C4-A, 'G' Block, Bandra-Kurla Complex, Bandra (East), Mumbai, Maharashtra - 400051
